.. _group___cmp_c_a_a_can_l2_itf___settings_1ga03391af5a8d95e965777830f2904919d:

#define CANL2KEY_INT_PERSISTENTBAUDRATE "PersistentBaudrate"
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

<type>Int</type>

Global setting for all CAN Networks. If 1 Baudrate used in DriverOpen will be saved to Net.X.DefaultBaudrate.

.. _group___cmp_c_a_a_can_l2_itf___settings_1gaf150d4b862d36afdf456c768c4394ed7:

<type>String</type>

Setting prefix for CANL2 Networks.

.. _group___cmp_c_a_a_can_l2_itf___settings_1gafb5151cddec9cb535bd9eddc639e5131:

#define CANL2KEY_INT_BAUDRATE "DefaultBaudrate"
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

<type>Int</type>

Default Baudrate in kbit/s which should be used if CAN interface will be opened with baudrate 0. Example: Net.0.Baudrate = 1000
